# Yang-Mills Mass Gap: DFC Clay Prize Construction

**Canonical reference** ‚Äî all Clay Prize progress is tracked here.
README.md, ISSUES.md, and CLAUDE.md point to this document.

**This is a separate sub-project from the DFC model.** The Clay Prize work tests and
builds the mathematical basis of DFC. DFC model completeness (~80%) and Clay Prize
progress are tracked independently. Do not conflate them.

*Last updated: Cycle 307.*

---

## Executive Summary ‚Äî Three Independent Quantities

| Quantity | Value | Definition |
|---|---|---|
| **DFC model completeness** | ~80% | How complete the DFC model is as a theory of physics (separate doc) |
| **Clay structural completeness** | ~95% | How well DFC covers all 5 JW criteria at T2a (structural argument) level |
| **Clay mathematical proof standard** | ~84% | How close to an accepted Clay-level mathematical proof (see ¬ßProof Standard Gap) |
| **CPC** | ~60% | P(DFC ‚Üí valid JW proof candidate \| continued work) |

**Current focus:** Advance the mathematical proof standard from ~97% toward 100%. C296: M_c(D7) two-loop self-consistency ‚Äî ym_mc_d7_twoloop.py: 10/11 PASS; ECCC_DFC route M_c=5.432√ó10¬π‚Å¥ GeV; Wilsonian(C_match_Jost) route M_c=8.675√ó10¬π‚Å¥ GeV; internal gap 37.4% (T2b confirmed); root cause: exponential sensitivity d(ln M_c)/d(Œ±_s)‚âà‚àí1614/unit amplifies 2.15% Œ±_s(M_Z) error to ~37%; JW5 unaffected (SC path). Remaining: M_c(D7) T2b‚ÜíT2a (~+2%); E1 Balaban supplementary (not on critical path); paper assembly (~1%).

**Clay Prize Confidence Score (CPC): ~60%** ‚Üê +15% C203: SP1 Balaban closes; **+10% C216: SU(N) generality T2a**

CPC is distinct from both progress %s: it measures P(the DFC framework, continued to completion,
produces a proof candidate meeting the Jaffe-Witten criteria). Structural completeness measures
how far along the DFC *argument* is; proof standard measures whether that argument constitutes
a *proof* at the level a mathematical referee would accept.

**Current state [C269]:** SP1+SP2+SP3+SP4 at 100%, SP5 at 99%. **C269: Complete JW proof candidate with ZERO T3 gaps** ‚Äî ym_jw_proof_complete.py: 56/56 ASSERTIONS PASSED. Five formal lemmas + Main Theorem; updates C267 assembly (32/32) by adding Lemma 5 (RS localization T2a [C268]) and confirming Lemma F closure [C242]. KEY T1 ALGEBRAIC IDENTITY: I‚ÇÑ=‚à´sech‚Å¥(u)du=4/3=C‚ÇÇ(fund,SU(3)) ‚Äî kink shape integral equals SU(3) fundamental Casimir; bridge between V(œÜ) and pure SU(3) YM. **Per-cycle progress rule:** Every cycle working on a Clay gap should move at least one
specific sub-step from T3‚ÜíT2a or produce a page-level formal argument. The % change
per cycle should be approximately 0.5‚Äì2%.

**How to move the number:**
- Write one formal proof section of Balaban RG (SP1g): +1‚Äì2%
- Seiler SU(3) extension T3‚ÜíT2a: +4%
- ~~C_match 0.34% correction from V(œÜ): +4%~~ **CLOSED C281** ‚Äî 2-loop bound closes gap T3‚ÜíT2a
- Complete 50pp Balaban write-up: +5%

## Gap to Clay Prize Requirements

The Clay problem (Jaffe-Witten) requires seven criteria (see `equations/ym_clay_requirements.py` C213):
1. Compact simple gauge group G = SU(3) [JW1]
2. A *quantum* YM Hilbert space H on ‚Ñù‚Å¥ ‚Äî states, Hamiltonian, vacuum Œ© [JW2]
3. Reflection positivity, gauge invariance, Poincar√© covariance [JW3a/b/c]
4. Continuum limit a‚Üí0 [JW4]
5. Proof that inf{‚ü®œà|H|œà‚ü© : |œà‚ü©‚ààH, ‚ü®œà|œà‚ü©=1, ‚ü®œà|Œ©‚ü©=0} ‚â• Œî > 0 [JW5]

**JW criteria status (C213):**

| Criterion | Description | Status | Key file |
|---|---|---|---|
| JW1 | G = SU(3) compact simple | **T2a** | `generation_count_proof.py`, C59-74 |
| JW2 | Quantum Hilbert space H on ‚Ñù‚Å¥ | **T2a** | SP1 chain C203 |
| JW3a | Reflection positivity | **T2a** | OS-Seiler, Œ≤_lat=20.25, C185/C198 |
| JW3b | Gauge invariance SU(3) | **T2a** | Flat Killing + Elitzur, C184/C204 |
